
### Eventually I would like differing states to have varying costs depending on whether they're a tunnel, or station.
### Making it more harder and more rewarding to explore rather than a random chance to win / lose. 
### Eventually this code may be made redudntant. And Scripted GUI used instead.

reclaim_metro = {

 	reclaim_2 = {
        icon = decision_generic_military
		cost = 20 ### Change Cost depending on type of abandoned state? 
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 20

        ai_will_do = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
            state = 2
        }
        visible = {
            RUI = {
                owns_state = 2
            }
            2 = {
                any_neighbor_state = {
                    is_controlled_by = ROOT
                }
            }
        }

		available = {
			2 = {
                is_owned_by = RUI
			}
			has_manpower > 10
			has_equipment = {
                infantry_equipment > 9
                supplies_equipment > 1
            }
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = reclaimation_underway 
				2 = {
					has_state_flag = state_being_colonised
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_manpower = -10
		    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		        type = infantry_equipment
		        amount = -10
		    }
		    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		        type = supplies_equipment
		        amount = -2
		    }
			set_country_flag = reclaimation_underway
			2 = {
				set_state_flag = state_being_colonised
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
		    random_list = {
		        50 = {
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.2
		            2 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
		        25 = { #Overwhelmed Mutants
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.mutants
		            2 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
		        25 = { #Expedition lost
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.lost
		            2 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
			}
			clr_country_flag = reclaimation_underway
		}
    }

		cost = 20 ### Change Cost depending on type of abandoned state? 
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 20

        ai_will_do = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
            state = 80
        }
        visible = {
            RUI = {
                owns_state = 80
            }
            80 = {
                any_neighbor_state = {
                    is_controlled_by = ROOT
                }
            }
        }

		available = {
			80 = {
                is_owned_by = RUI
			}
			has_manpower > 10
			has_equipment = {
                infantry_equipment > 9
                supplies_equipment > 1
            }
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = reclaimation_underway 
				80 = {
					has_state_flag = state_being_colonised
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_manpower = -10
		    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		        type = infantry_equipment
		        amount = -10
		    }
		    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		        type = supplies_equipment
		        amount = -2
		    }
			set_country_flag = reclaimation_underway
			80 = {
				set_state_flag = state_being_colonised
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
		    random_list = {
		        50 = {
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.80
		            10 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
		        25 = { #Overwhelmed Mutants
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.mutants
		            10 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
		        25 = { #Expedition lost
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.lost
		            80 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
			}
			clr_country_flag = reclaimation_underway
		}
    }

		cost = 20 ### Change Cost depending on type of abandoned state? 
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 20

        ai_will_do = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
            state = 437
        }
        visible = {
            RUI = {
                owns_state = 437
            }
            437 = {
                any_neighbor_state = {
                    is_controlled_by = ROOT
                }
            }
        }

		available = {
			437 = {
                is_owned_by = RUI
			}
			has_manpower > 10
			has_equipment = {
                infantry_equipment > 9
                supplies_equipment > 1
            }
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = reclaimation_underway 
				437 = {
					has_state_flag = state_being_colonised
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_manpower = -10
		    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		        type = infantry_equipment
		        amount = -10
		    }
		    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		        type = supplies_equipment
		        amount = -2
		    }
			set_country_flag = reclaimation_underway
			437 = {
				set_state_flag = state_being_colonised
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
		    random_list = {
		        50 = {
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.437
		            437 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
		        25 = { #Overwhelmed Mutants
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.mutants
		            437 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
		        25 = { #Expedition lost
		            country_event = reclaimation_event.lost
		            437 = {
						clr_state_flag = state_being_colonised
					}
		        }
			}
			clr_country_flag = reclaimation_underway
		}
    }
